- "Passkeys are digital keys saved to your iCloud Keychain. They are backed up and sync across all of your Apple devices. You can use a passkey to sign in to apps and websites on iPhone, iPad, Mac, Apple TV, Vision\u00a0Pro, and web browsers on other platforms.\n\nPasskeys keep your accounts more secure than passwords do. They use powerful cryptography, which makes every passkey strong. Unlike passwords, malicious websites cannot trick you into giving away your passkeys.\n\nYou sign in to apps and websites with passkeys differently than you do with passwords. When prompted to sign in with a passkey, you use Face ID, Touch ID, Optic\u00a0ID, or your device passcode. Your biometric information and device passcode are never sent to the service you’re signing in to.\n\nYou can use AirDrop to share accounts with people in your contacts."
